I would HIGHLY recommend finding a great moisturizer to use to apply to the area to prevent the area from becoming too dry, especially if your skin is very sensitive. I personally like to use Cetaphil moisturizing fragrance free lotion (you can find for under $10) or sometimes I like to use a little BIO OIL when I have it (BIO OIL, is about $5-$10 for a 2 fl oz bottle, but has proven to me to be VERY effective in moisturizing and great for a variety of skin problems).<br />I think the main things you should make sure of when choosing a moisturizer is that it's (1) fragrance free, as this can sometimes cause more problems for skin prone to razor bumps, and (2) not too heavy, as this can clog pores and also make matters worse. Just make sure that you keep the area properly hydrated.<br /><br />Also on my off days, when I don't shave, I'll still apply a little TENDSKIN after washing my face before bed.<br /><br />Personally, the smell really isn't that bad if you use it correctly, and it's nothing that can't be covered with some cheap cologne/perfume. BUT if the smell is really that much of an issue for you, I would either only shave at night and put this on before bed, OR I would recommend trying Barc Bump down razor relief cream.<br />This cream is the only other product I've used that works to remove and prevent razor bumps. It's a little bit more pricey than TENDSKIN not by much though, but it doesn't have a strong scent at all. It's very creamy and goes on like a light lotion and it also doesn't dry the skin out as much.
